        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/432706794?book_show_action=true">Oct 12, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Yesi ~ LLL" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Yesi ~ LLL" href="/user/show/9324901-yesi-lll">Yesi ~ LLL</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer432706794" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9630386652970915183">After thinking about it for a couple of days my rating has been bumped up. ~ The first half of the book was good although I thought Jack and Cassie got together too quickly. The second half of the book, about 60% in, made me so sick that I wanted to jump in my iPad and punch Jack! What he did, and he knew exactly what he was doing, was just so awful my heart broke. Seriously my heart was racing the entire time and then it was shattered. The way he handled the situation...EVEN WORSE! I hated him </span>
  <span id="freeText9630386652970915183" style="display:none">After thinking about it for a couple of days my rating has been bumped up. ~ The first half of the book was good although I thought Jack and Cassie got together too quickly. The second half of the book, about 60% in, made me so sick that I wanted to jump in my iPad and punch Jack! What he did, and he knew exactly what he was doing, was just so awful my heart broke. Seriously my heart was racing the entire time and then it was shattered. The way he handled the situation...EVEN WORSE! I hated him and the other person involved even though he was trying to do "the right thing". UGH! I thought he was the biggest jerk for what he did and the biggest idiot for how he handled it! Cassie was stupid for begging and for how quickly all was forgiven. The ending ALMOST made up for the horrible angst the second half of the book gave me. Overall, it was a great read! I would recommend it if you like baseball, a HOT baseball player, college romance, and an angst filled read with some funny moments and a love conquers all tone to it. The secondary characters, Melissa and Dean were fantastic and I hope we get their stories too. Any book that makes have all kinds of emotions is definitely worth the read and a 4+star rating! Read it!!! </span>
  <a data-text-id="9630386652970915183" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_511139987" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/511139987" />
    <a title="RomanceAddict" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3153958-romanceaddict"><img alt="RomanceAddict" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/f_50x66-6a03a5c12233c941481992b82eea8d23.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/511139987?book_show_action=true">Jan 19, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="RomanceAddict" class="user" itemprop="url" name="RomanceAddict" href="/user/show/3153958-romanceaddict">RomanceAddict</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer511139987" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16330218334461861996">SPOILER AHEAD!<br/>Okay honestly, I just need to vent, because wow, this book made me angry. I really wanted to enjoy this story, especially given the rave reviews which I can still NOT even understand. Please just tell me: since WHEN IS CHEATING SEXY? What he did was unforgivable. And then he wants to do the right (and stupid) thing and marry the girl he got pregnant? The H and H deserve each other. He cheated and hardly even tried to win her back, and then she practically goes beg him not to leave </span>
  <span id="freeText16330218334461861996" style="display:none">SPOILER AHEAD!<br />Okay honestly, I just need to vent, because wow, this book made me angry. I really wanted to enjoy this story, especially given the rave reviews which I can still NOT even understand. Please just tell me: since WHEN IS CHEATING SEXY? What he did was unforgivable. And then he wants to do the right (and stupid) thing and marry the girl he got pregnant? The H and H deserve each other. He cheated and hardly even tried to win her back, and then she practically goes beg him not to leave her. If she's stupid enough to beg him to come back to her even after what he did and plans to marry someone else, and if he's stupid and cowardly enough to cheat on her and then believe he'll be a better guy because he's going to marry her? Yeah they deserve each other. The only balls that boy has are the ones he plays with on the field, clearly. Also the book has practically zero plot until the point where he actually goes out and cheat in the middle. Everything before it, it's just the H/H trying to have a relationship thinking and worrying that he's going to screw up. Guess what? He did. Very disappointing book. </span>
  <a data-text-id="16330218334461861996" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<script type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8">
//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('jL0uq0Ek2swI0KoY+Aryj8MSdNd5uSPet2SXaVrZMSX121djFeX//R0cE+tTgt2VT6GHJ0rJxKznyWP+bdDYYg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('KVETKB0NDAP1iN/I+R58YNJVB2sK/VooQNY8TZd9YQBQN2rgScwpMuBEZjtSllN6Xub0mzmNvVoQe8jaoHSIRw==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

  <span id="freeText11886913836945755062" style="display:none">J. (jenn) Sterling is a New York Times and USA Today best selling author of multiple contemporary romances.
